[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA medium-severity Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m issue was detected by the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer fuzzer harness when parsing XLIFF data. During XML parsing, an external [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity reference triggered an outbound connection to “jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m,” which was [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflagged by the `ServerSideRequestForgery` sanitizer. The report indicates that [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted XML input can lead to unauthorized network requests.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing run on the XLIFF parser produced a [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: Server Side Request [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mForgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` exception. The fuzzer input caused the XML parser to attempt an [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutbound TCP connection to “jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m.” This behavior was intercepted by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf`, demonstrating that the parser will follow and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolve external entity references or other network-fetchable constructs based on [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted data.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant observations and findings:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The exception arises in `ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf` and [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`checkSsrfSocket`, indicating that the runtime sanitizer has flagged the socket [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnect call.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace shows the flow from `java.net.Socket.connect` through the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuilt-in JDK HTTP client [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`HttpClient.openServer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, into the Xerces XML entity [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanager [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XMLEntityManager.setupCurrentEntity`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and ultimately into the XLIFF [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.tika.parser.xliff.XLIFF12Parser`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XliffParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invokes `SAXParser.parse` on untrusted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput, which triggers entity resolution logic within the XML parser.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The root of the network request is the parser’s handling of external entities or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDTDs during the SAX parsing of XLIFF content.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo fully understand the scope of this SSRF issue, the following parts of the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase should be investigated:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The configuration and usage of the XML parser [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`javax.xml.parsers.SAXParserFactory` and any features or properties set on the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `XLIFF12Parser._parse` and related methods.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The logic in `XLIFF12Parser` that reads or processes external entities, DTD [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferences, or any constructs that lead to network access.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `ServerSideRequestForgery` sanitizer implementation in [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers`, particularly the checks performed in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`checkSsrf` and `checkSsrfSocket`.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer harness entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XliffParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to confirm how input is fed [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto the parser and whether entity resolution is enabled by default.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo assumptions have been made about underlying causes beyond what is evident in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack trace and sanitizer output. This evaluation focuses on the observable SSRF [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior and highlights the code areas relevant for further analysis.[0m               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The SSRF arises because [0m[1;35mXLIFF12Parser._parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses a plain [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which by default allows external entity resolution [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g. external-general-entities, external-parameter-entities, loading external [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDTDs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. When the parser encounters an external entity reference in an XLIFF file, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Xerces XMLEntityManager opens a TCP connection to resolve it, triggering the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF sanitizer.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;35mXLIFF12Parser._parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m currently only sets namespace awareness and proceeds [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, handler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. We must preserve namespace-aware, non-validating [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing, the use of CloseShieldInputStream [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif used later[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and the [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDefaultHandler-[0m[35m/[0m[95mParseContext-driven[0m[39m content handling.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not touch any fuzz harness or tests; only modify XLIFF12Parser.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Recommended Fix[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Delegate parser configuration to the existing secure XML parsing utility in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Tika codebase: [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.getSAXParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.tika.utils.XMLReaderUtils`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This factory already applies the following[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhardening:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • XMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING = true  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • external-general-entities = false  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • external-parameter-entities = false  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • load-external-dtd = false  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • load-dtd-grammar = false  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the manual factory creation and parser instantiation in [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mXLIFF12Parser._parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with either:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m A direct call to [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, or  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m A call to [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.getSAXParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m followed by [0m[1;35mnewSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand [0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Proposal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mapproach a, more concise[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     import org.apache.tika.utils.XMLReaderUtils;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static void [0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is, DefaultHandler contentHandler,[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                ParseContext context[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             throws SAXException, IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         CloseShieldInputStream safeIs = [0m[1;35mCloseShieldInputStream.wrap[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeIs, contentHandler, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This one-line change [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter imports[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m immediately applies the secure features [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand maintains the existing handler/context contract.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `XLIFF12Parser.java`:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Add import:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `import org.apache.tika.utils.XMLReaderUtils;`[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In method `[0m[1;35m_parse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, remove lines [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m89[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe manual factory and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Insert:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        CloseShieldInputStream safeIs = [0m[1;35mCloseShieldInputStream.wrap[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[39msafeIs, contentHandler, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove redundant `[0m[1;35mfactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call since [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.getSAXParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` already does that.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure `CloseShieldInputStream` is imported [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready is on line [0m[1;36m28[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach reuses a tested, centralized XML parsing utility that uniformly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menforces secure processing across Tika parsers.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It eliminates SSRF by disabling all external entity resolution and DTD [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloading, satisfying the sanitizer checks without broad exception handling or [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maltering‐harness code.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It preserves namespace awareness, non-validating parsing, and the existing SAX[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mevent flow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia DefaultHandler/ParseContext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar pattern is already used in `XMLParser.java`, so this change aligns [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXLIFF parsing with the rest of the codebase.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Validation & Side Effects[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing XLIFF parser unit tests to confirm no regressions in internal [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing logic.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Manually verify that valid inline entities in XLIFF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnon-external[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m still parse[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly [0m[1;39m([0m[39minternal entities are unaffected[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If any legitimate use of external DTDs was relied upon, document the change in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelease notes; typically Tika discourages external DTD resolution for security.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to fuzz harness, test code, or external dependencies are required.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar secure parsing in `org.apache.tika.parser.xml.XMLParser` via [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.getSAXParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` feature flags at lines [0m[1;36m218[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m234[0m[39m in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XMLReaderUtils.java`.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XLIFF12Parser`, as untrusted XML content triggered an HTTP connection. To mitigate[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception org.apache.tika.exception.TikaException; must be caught or declared to be[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A Jazzer fuzzer run produced a `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: Server Side Request [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mForgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` exception.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace originates in XML parsing of XLIFF data [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`XliffParserFuzzer.parseOne` → `XLIFF12Parser._parse`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ultimately invoking [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This indicates that external entity resolution or network access during XML [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing can be influenced by untrusted input.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `XLIFF12Parser.java` under [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-parser-xml-module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/xliff/`:  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Removed the `SAXParserFactory` instantiation and `[0m[1;35mfactory.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincoming `InputStream` with `[0m[1;35mCloseShieldInputStream.wrap[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.parseSAX[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The error states that `org.apache.tika.exception.TikaException` is thrown by [0m     [2m                [0m
